<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">On August&#160;11, 2022 we issued the press release furnished as Exhibit 99.1. The press release describes the results of our operations for the quarter and fiscal year ended June&#160;30, 2022. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The information furnished in this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> under Item 2.02 and the attached exhibit shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;8.01. Other Events. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">On August&#160;11, 2022 we announced that our board of directors declared a quarterly cash dividend of US $0.44 per share. The dividend will have a record date of August&#160;18, 2022, payable on September&#160;22, 2022. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#8217;s common stock trading on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of CHESS Depositary Instruments trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. The <span style="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</span> date will be August&#160;17, 2022, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#8217;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from August&#160;17, 2022, through August&#160;18, 2022, inclusive.</p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Exhibits </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>ResMed Inc. Announces Results for the Fourth Quarter of Fiscal Year 2022 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#150; <I>Year-over-year revenue grows 4%, operating profit up 6%, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating profit up 4%</I> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>&#150; Quarterly dividend increases 5% to $0.44 per share </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Note: A webcast of ResMed&#146;s conference call will be available at 4:30 p.m. ET today at&nbsp;<U>http://investor.resmed.com</U> </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">SAN DIEGO, August&nbsp;11, 2022 &#150; ResMed Inc. (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) today announced results for its quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Fourth Quarter 2022 Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>All comparisons are to the prior year
period </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Revenue increased by 4% to $914.7&nbsp;million; up 8% on a constant currency basis</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Gross margin grew 110 bps to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">57.1%;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross</FONT> margin grew 50 bps to
57.8% </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Diluted earnings per share of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">$1.33;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> earnings per share
of $1.49 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Full Year 2022 Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>All comparisons
are to the prior year period </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Revenue increased by 12% to $3.6&nbsp;billion; up 13% on a constant currency basis</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Gross margin contracted 90 bps to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">56.6%;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross</FONT> margin contracted
140 bps to 57.7% </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Income from operations increased <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">11%;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;operating</FONT> profit up 8%
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Diluted earnings per share of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">$5.30;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> earnings per share
of $5.79 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Our fourth quarter and full-year fiscal year 2022 results demonstrate strong growth and ResMed&#146;s market leadership,&#148;
said Mick Farrell, ResMed&#146;s CEO. &#147;During the quarter, we saw continued adoption of our most advanced platform innovation to date, the 100% cloud-connectable AirSense 11. We launched this solution into several new countries in Europe while
continuing to see strong sales in the U.S. We also introduced our newest device to meet the needs of an industry crisis in PAP supply, the AirSense 10 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Card-to-Cloud</FONT></FONT>
solution, during the quarter. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">card-to-cloud</FONT></FONT> device was launched into the U.S. and many other markets and is designed to work without an embedded communications
module. This redesign allowed us to increase deliveries to customers and ultimately get many more patients onto life-saving sleep apnea and respiratory care therapy. Both of these platforms, as well as our legacy, market-leading, 100%
cloud-connected AirSense 10 device, will support solid growth throughout FY23. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">


<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" ALIGN="center">

<TD WIDTH="89%"></TD>

<TD WIDTH="9%"></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"><I>RMD Fourth Quarter 2022 Earnings Press Release &#150; August 11, 2022</I></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ALIGN="right"><I>Page&nbsp;</I><B><I>
 2
&nbsp;</I></B><I>of&nbsp;</I><B><I>10</I></B><I></I></TD></TR></TABLE> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;I am incredibly proud of the global ResMed team that was able to deliver strong constant currency revenue growth
of 8% in the June quarter. During the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2022, we annualized $20&nbsp;million in COVID-related ventilator sales and incremental revenue in the range of $60 to $70&nbsp;million related to a competitor&#146;s recall during
the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2021. For full fiscal year 2022, we achieved $3.6&nbsp;billion in revenue, with 13% constant currency revenue growth year-over-year, and operating profit growth of 8%, all on a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Our global team remains focused on supporting patients, providers, and physicians &#150; our top
priority is to get products directly into the hands of patients who need therapy most. Looking ahead, we are confident in our ability to grow steadily throughout fiscal year 2023 and to continue delivering for all stakeholders. We are investing in
R&amp;D to drive accelerated adoption of digital health solutions in sleep apnea, COPD, and outside-hospital care, as we progress towards our goal to improve 250&nbsp;million lives in 2025.&#148; </P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">In order to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of foreign
currency fluctuations, we provide certain financial information on a &#147;constant currency&#148; basis, which is in addition to the actual financial information presented. In order to calculate our constant currency information, we translate the
current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to U.S. dollar
measures that reflect current period exchange rates, or to other financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>Discussion of Fourth Quarter Results </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>All comparisons are to the prior year period unless otherwise noted </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Revenue grew by 8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, driven by increased demand for our sleep and respiratory care
devices and reduced competitive supply. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Revenue in the U.S., Canada, and Latin America, excluding
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Software-as-a-Service,</FONT></FONT></FONT> grew by 12&nbsp;percent, primarily due to the factors discussed above and recovery of core sleep patient
flow that was previously impacted by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19.</FONT> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Revenue in Europe, Asia, and other markets grew by 1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Excluding the impact of
COVID-related sales in the prior year quarter, revenue grew by 8% on a constant currency basis, primarily due to the factors discussed above. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Software-as-a-Service revenue increased by 8&nbsp;percent, due to continued growth in our Durable Medical Equipment
category and stabilizing patient flow in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> care settings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Gross margin increased by 110 basis points and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross margin increased by
50 basis points, mainly due to an increase in average selling prices and favorable product mix changes, partially offset by higher freight and manufacturing costs, and unfavorable geographic mix changes. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Selling, general, and administrative expenses increased by 12&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. SG&amp;A expenses
increased to 21.3&nbsp;percent of revenue in the quarter, compared with 20.7&nbsp;percent in the same period of the prior year. These changes in SG&amp;A expenses were mainly due to increases in employee-related expenses, increases in professional
service fees, including acquisition-related expenses, and increases in travel expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

operations increased by 4&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> net income increased by 10&nbsp;percent to $219.2&nbsp;million and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share increased by 10&nbsp;percent to $1.49, predominantly
attributable to strong sales, partially offset by higher operating expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> software solutions for providers in major settings across the care continuum, from Hg, a leading software and services investor. Under the agreement
terms, ResMed will acquire MEDIFOX DAN for approximately US$1.0&nbsp;billion (<FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#128;</FONT>950 million), which ResMed expects to fund with its existing credit facilities. The transaction is expected to close
by the end of the second quarter of ResMed&#146;s fiscal year 2023 (December 31, 2022), subject to regulatory clearances. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>Dividend program </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The ResMed board of directors today declared a
quarterly cash dividend of $0.44 per share. The dividend will have a record date of August&nbsp;18, 2022, payable on September&nbsp;22, 2022. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#146;s common stock trading on the New York
Stock Exchange. Holders of CHESS Depositary Interests (&#147;CDIs&#148;) trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1
ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;ex-dividend&nbsp;date</FONT> will be August&nbsp;17, 2022, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#146;s settlement
operating rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from August&nbsp;17, 2022, through August&nbsp;18, 2022, inclusive.</P>

2022 results on its webcast at 1:30 p.m. U.S. Pacific Time today. The live webcast of the call can be accessed on ResMed&#146;s Investor Relations website at <U>investor.resmed.com</U>. Please go to this section of the website and click on the icon
for the &#147;Q4 2022 Earnings Webcast&#148; to register and listen to the live webcast. A replay of the earnings webcast will be accessible on the website and available approximately two hours after the live webcast. In addition, a telephone replay
of the conference call will be available approximately two hours after the webcast by dialing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">+1&nbsp;877-660-6853&nbsp;(U.S.)</FONT></FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">+1&nbsp;201-612-7415&nbsp;(outside</FONT></FONT> U.S.) and entering the passcode 13731513. The telephone replay will be available until August&nbsp;25, 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>About ResMed </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">At ResMed (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) we pioneer innovative
solutions that treat and keep people out of the hospital, empowering them to live healthier, higher-quality lives. Our digital health technologies and cloud-connected medical devices transform care for people with sleep apnea, COPD, and other
chronic diseases. Our comprehensive <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> software platforms support the professionals and caregivers who help people stay healthy in the home or care setting
of their choice. By enabling better care, we improve quality of life, reduce the impact of chronic disease, and lower costs for consumers and healthcare systems in more than 140 countries. To learn more, visit <U>ResMed.com</U> and follow @ResMed.

to materially differ from those projected or implied in the forward-looking statements. Additional risks and uncertainties are discussed in ResMed&#146;s periodic reports on file with the U.S. Securities&nbsp;&amp; Exchange Commission. ResMed does

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">ResMed adjusts for the impact of the amortization of acquired intangibles, acquisition-related expenses, reserve for
disputed tax positions, restructuring expenses and the (gain) loss on equity investments from their evaluation of ongoing operations, and believes that investors benefit from adjusting these items to facilitate a more meaningful evaluation of
current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">ResMed believes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">that&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> earnings
per share is an additional measure of performance that investors can use to compare operating results between reporting periods. ResMed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">uses&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;information</FONT> internally in planning, forecasting,
and evaluating the results of operations in the current period and in comparing it to past periods. ResMed believes this information provides investors better insight when evaluating ResMed&#146;s performance from core operations and provides
consistent financial reporting. The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> is intended to supplement, and not to replace, the presentation of net income and other GAAP measures. Like
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;earnings</FONT></FONT> are subject to inherent limitations because they do not include all the expenses that must be included under
GAAP. </P>

current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to U.S. dollar

e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
